Additionally, you can check case status through the online case status feature on the Supreme Court website.\n\n## Mobile Access\n\nFor those preferring mobile access, the Supreme Court of Pakistan app helps lawyers track proceedings and can be accessed by registering with a verified mobile number, or even as a guest user.\n\nThe main website domains for accessing this information are scp.gov.pk and supremecourt.gov.pk.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"uuid":"a8e6b690-1c68-49ee-b95a-37d30409c037","timestamp":"2026-03-08T01:30:06.307Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"02cb1c99-5cb4-431d-8b3c-ebb066f76809"}

Each provincial high court has developed its own system for accessing judgments and case information:\n\n**Individual High Court Portals:**\n\n- The Peshawar High Court's web application facilitates stakeholders with file status checks and daily ordersheets/judgment files, allowing users to search registered case files along with case file contents including daily order sheets and judgments.\n\n- The Peshawar High Court's Abbottabad Bench provides a web application that facilitates stakeholders with file status check and daily ordersheets/judgment files, allowing litigants to view their case files through web browsers and mobile devices from anywhere in the world.\n\n- The Islamabad High Court has subscriptions to online legal databases including Pakistan law site (case law of Pakistani Superior Courts) and PLJ Law Site, with latest orders and judgments also accessible through the IHC website.\n\n- The Lahore High Court maintains a \"Judgments Approved for Reporting\" section on its data portal.\n\n**Comprehensive Legal Databases:**\n\nUnreported judgments from SCP, LHC, SHC, IHC, BHC, AJK SC, AJK HC, and PHC are available through platforms like Pak Legal Database.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"uuid":"16503876-1c9d-441d-973e-168673efc56e","timestamp":"2026-03-08T01:30:09.263Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"0d3b86f2-7645-45e6-9359-5fbf557b91d5"}
